and removes members when they stop sending heartbeats.\\n\\n## Configuration Definition\\nThe heartbeat session timeout threshold is defined through the configuration parameter `SESSION_TIMEOUT_MS_CONFIG` in `CommonClientConfigs.java`. This configuration is extracted into `GroupRebalanceConfig.java` (line 41) which stores the `sessionTimeoutMs` value (line 52).\\n\\n## Client-Side Timeout Detection\\nOn the consumer client side, the `Heartbeat.java` class manages heartbeat timing. The `sessionTimeoutExpired()` method (lines 119-122) checks whether the session timer has expired by calling `sessionTimer.isExpired()`. This method is invoked during the consumer polling loop in the heartbeat thread.\\n\\nThe heartbeat timeout check occurs in `AbstractCoordinator.java` within the `HeartbeatThread.run()` method (lines 1513-1517). When `heartbeat.sessionTimeoutExpired(now)` returns true, the client marks the coordinator as unknown with the message \\\"session timed out without receiving a heartbeat response\\\". This causes the consumer group membership to drop as the client can no longer communicate with the group coordinator.\\n\\n## Server-Side Timeout Handling\\nOn the broker/group coordinator side, `GroupMetadataManager.java` implements `expireClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat()` (lines 6664-6702) which is invoked when a member's heartbeat session timeout expires. This method removes the member from the group and logs: \\\"Member {memberId} in group {groupId} has failed, removing it from the group\\\" (lines 6691-6692) or \\\"Pending member {memberId} in group {groupId} has been removed after session timeout expiration\\\" (lines 6682-6683).\\n\\n## Call Chain\\nThe complete flow is:\\n1. `Heartbeat.sessionTimeoutExpired()` detects the timeout on the client side\\n2. `AbstractCoordinator.HeartbeatThread.run()` detects this and calls `markCoordinatorUnknown()`\\n3. The consumer drops group membership\\n4. Server-side: `GroupMetadataManager.expireClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat()` removes the member and triggers rebalancing\\n\\nThe timeout value is controlled by the `session.timeout.ms` configuration (default 10 seconds), which must be set according to broker constraints defined by `group.min.session.timeout.ms` and `group.max.session.timeout.ms`.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":9073,"cache_read_input_tokens":86326,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":9073},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"eae0fe5f-2499-47e2-b893-9d378a2a1765","uuid":"8346a7c4-bf0a-4205-a27e-839b7fab7c0a"}

and removes members when they stop sending heartbeats.\\n\\n## Configuration Definition\\nThe heartbeat session timeout threshold is defined through the configuration parameter `SESSION_TIMEOUT_MS_CONFIG` in `CommonClientConfigs.java`. This configuration is extracted into `GroupRebalanceConfig.java` (line 41) which stores the `sessionTimeoutMs` value (line 52).\\n\\n## Client-Side Timeout Detection\\nOn the consumer client side, the `Heartbeat.java` class manages heartbeat timing. The `sessionTimeoutExpired()` method (lines 119-122) checks whether the session timer has expired by calling `sessionTimer.isExpired()`. This method is invoked during the consumer polling loop in the heartbeat thread.\\n\\nThe heartbeat timeout check occurs in `AbstractCoordinator.java` within the `HeartbeatThread.run()` method (lines 1513-1517). When `heartbeat.sessionTimeoutExpired(now)` returns true, the client marks the coordinator as unknown with the message \\\"session timed out without receiving a heartbeat response\\\". This causes the consumer group membership to drop as the client can no longer communicate with the group coordinator.\\n\\n## Server-Side Timeout Handling\\nOn the broker/group coordinator side, `GroupMetadataManager.java` implements `expireClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat()` (lines 6664-6702) which is invoked when a member's heartbeat session timeout expires. This method removes the member from the group and logs: \\\"Member {memberId} in group {groupId} has failed, removing it from the group\\\" (lines 6691-6692) or \\\"Pending member {memberId} in group {groupId} has been removed after session timeout expiration\\\" (lines 6682-6683).\\n\\n## Call Chain\\nThe complete flow is:\\n1. `Heartbeat.sessionTimeoutExpired()` detects the timeout on the client side\\n2. `AbstractCoordinator.HeartbeatThread.run()` detects this and calls `markCoordinatorUnknown()`\\n3. The consumer drops group membership\\n4. Server-side: `GroupMetadataManager.expireClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat()` removes the member and triggers rebalancing\\n\\nThe timeout value is controlled by the `session.timeout.ms` configuration (default 10 seconds), which must be set according to broker constraints defined by `group.min.session.timeout.ms` and `group.max.session.timeout.ms`.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
